                <header class="blog_entry-header">
                  <div class="blog_entry-header-inner">
                    <h2 class="blog_entry-title"> <a rel="bookmark" href="https://www.lawyersnjurists.com/lawyer_ci/digest/bankruptcy-act---civil-rules-and-orders">BANKRUPTCY ACT - CIVIL RULES AND ORDERS</a> </h2>
                  </div>
                  <!--blog_entry-header-inner--> 
                </header>
                <div class="entry-content">
                  <div class="entry-content">
                    <p><b>Subject:</b>  BANKRUPTCY ACT - CIVIL</p>
                    <p><b>Case Year:</b>  </p>
                    <p><b>Relevant Law:</b>  BANKRUPTCY ACT - CIVIL RULES AND ORDERS</p>
                    <p><b>Relevant Section:</b>  Rule 3, 207, 208, Section 74, Section 3, Section 9, Section 5 </p>
                    <p><b>Citation:</b>  21 BLD (AD) 119, 19 BLD (HCD) 281, 21 BLD (AD) 1, 21 BLD (HCD) 127, 14 BLD (AD) 81, 19 BLD (HCD) 129, 16 BLD (HCD) 5, 16 BLD (HCD) 303, 15 BLD (HCD) 155, 13 BLD (AD) 155, 22 BLD (HCD) 365, 20 BLD (HCD) 537, 48DLR(AD) 180, 18 BLD (AD) 33, 19 BLD (AD) 9, 2</p>

                    <h2 class="blog_entry-title"> <a rel="bookmark" href="https://www.lawyersnjurists.com/lawyer_ci/digest/constitution-of-bangladesh-1972-article-1---100">Constitution Of Bangladesh, 1972 [Article 1 - 100]</a> </h2>
